Guangdong Province's Progress in Civilizing the Li People

The provincial government plans to establish three more counties in Li territory and seeks to assimilate the Han and Li peoples through cultural means.

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Li and Miao peoples were originally indigenous to Guangdong and Guangxi. After the southward migration of the Han people, the Li and Miao in Guangxi retreated to Bapai, and those in Guangdong retreated to Qiongya (Hainan Island). Later, the Han people re-entered Qiongya, and the Li people retreated further inland. The thirteen counties now established along the coast of Qiongya are almost entirely inhabited by Han people. Although the land inhabited by the Li people is still under the jurisdiction of various counties, due to inconvenient transportation and differences in customs and language, the Li people are strong and fierce, making it impossible for the county government to implement any policies, thus creating a lawless situation. The Li people number over 500,000 and are divided into various groups: the Xiao Li, Xiao Xi, Li Chan, Sheng Tie Li, Da Bian Li, Hei Chan Li, Titou Li, and Miao people. The Li people often rely on their strength to bully the weak, commit violence against the few, and kill each other. Those who live close to the Han people often resort to violence over minor matters, killing and looting as if it were commonplace. If the government tries to enforce the law, they often harbor resentment, and the cunning ones take the opportunity to cause trouble. Therefore, after repeated suppression, it is ultimately difficult to quell them. Furthermore, the methods of governing the Li people in the past only sought to restrain them, rather than assimilate them with the Han people, making it difficult to achieve long-term peace and stability. Since implementing the three-year administration plan, the provincial government has been pacifying the regions and, after gradually suppressing the bandits and communists in Qiongya, has begun working to civilize the Li people. A commissioner for pacifying the Li people and a Li Affairs Bureau have been established to oversee the pacification. The commissioner for Qiongya, Chen Hanguang, previously accompanied over a hundred Lu Tong Li and Miao people from various tribes to Guangzhou for sightseeing and sent many Li and Miao people to the Yantang Military and Political School, other schools in Guangzhou, and various schools in Qiongya run by the provincial and local governments to study. The provincial government has also allocated educational funds to establish schools in Li territory, actively seeking to assimilate them. However, the work of pacifying the Li people is extremely difficult. Recently, the commissioner for pacifying the Li people has been abolished, and the Li Affairs Bureau is only a temporary organization and too small in scale. The bureau will also be abolished. However, in order to actively civilize the Li people, the provincial government plans to establish three more counties within their territory: (1) Establish a county to be named Le'an, with the county government located in Le'an, from the following areas of Changjiang County: Qiyi, Gan [illegible], Dongfang, Ma [illegible], Eyi, Eni, Zheinei Dong, Tianzhong, [illegible]gang and from the following areas of Yanan County: Le'an, Duojian Dong, Baoshan Dong, Baokang Dong, Longbi, Tanzhai, Duogang Dong, Toutang, Wanchong Dong, Fanyang Dong; and set up two assistant commissioner offices in Dongfang, Baozhao Dong. (2) Establish a county to be named Baoting, with the county government located in Baoshi, from the following areas of Yaxian County: Buda, Daluo, Shougang, Sangong, Baolong Dong, Zhoujia Dong, Shuiman Dong, Man Dong; from the following areas of Lingshui County: Baoshi, Wugong, Liugong, Qigong, Wuyadong, Lingmen Tuan, Baishi Tuan, Wuzhi Shan, Fenjie Ling, Diaoluo Shan; from the following areas of Wanning County: Shuisi, Nanhai Qiao, Xidong, Beidong; from the following areas of Lehui County: Zhugen Dong, Taiping Dong, Qiejie Dong, Heshui Tuan; and from the following areas of Ding'an County: Chuanbu, Nanyin Tuan, Jia Dong Tuan, Muri Shan; and set up two assistant commissioner offices in Zhugen Dong and Baishi Tuan. (3) Establish a county to be named Baisha, with the county government located in Baisha, from the following areas of Danxian County: Yayi Dong, Baisha Dong, Yuanmen Dong, Longtou Dong, Bingbang; from the following areas of Changjiang County: Bawang Dong, Wulie, Dapo, Baoping, Fengxu Dong; from the following areas of Gan'en County: Wushi Dong; from the following areas of Lingshui County: Nanliu Dong, Shiwan Dong; from the following areas of Ding'an County: Xinshi Ying, Genpu, Jia Chai Dong, Xiaoshui Dong, Sihe Dong; from the following areas of Yaxian County: Hongmao Shang Dong, Hongxia Dong, Daocai, Hongmao Cun; and from the following areas of Qiongshan County: Jialu Dong, Linwan Dong; and set up two assistant commissioner offices in Xinshi Ying and Bawang Dong. In the initial stages of establishing these three counties, the administration will be simple, and the county government organization and administrative expenses will differ from other counties. The county government organization will consist of one county magistrate, four assistant commissioners, three technicians, four clerks, four employees, four police chiefs, forty police officers, and eight yamen runners. Each county will receive monthly expenses of 1,700 yuan and a one-time construction fee of 500 yuan, and each county will receive 10,000 yuan for the construction of the county government and the assistant commissioner's offices. Educational funds have already been allocated, but since there is no local revenue, they will be disbursed from the provincial treasury. After the establishment of the county governments, in addition to governing the Li people and assimilating them through cultural means, they will actively build roads, reclaim land, teach the Li people various production techniques, and improve their living conditions and customs. This plan has been drafted by the Department of Civil Affairs and submitted to the provincial government for approval and will be implemented soon.

Songjiang: Bandit Attempted Robbery at Jinshanwei Unsuccessful

Jinshanwei in Punan is a small coastal town under the jurisdiction of the eighth district of this county, where theft cases often occur. Early in the morning (30th), more than thirty bandits, carrying seven or eight rifles and speaking in mixed accents, came from the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway. They broke into Jiang Zhenxing's fish shop and robbed it. Zhang Xiaomei in the shop was beaten on the forehead by the bandits, and more than four hundred yuan were lost. Then they went to Qi Dague's rice shop and robbed more than three hundred yuan. Then they went to Wu Qisheng's store to rob, but the owner, Wu, escaped. At this time, the town police rang the gong to warn the town, and the villagers gathered upon hearing the sound and shouted to catch the thieves. The bandits dared not stay any longer and fired several shots as a warning, then fled east along the original road. The victims have not yet reported to the county to request an arrest. However, not long after the Jiangzhuang robbery, although Jinshanwei was fortunate enough not to be robbed, the villagers are all worried.

Suzhou: County Government Takes Over the Bureau of Official Properties

The matters relating to official properties in the four counties of Wuxian, Kunshan, Wujiang, and Changshu were originally handled by the Bureau of Official Properties of Wu, Kun, Jiang, and Chang. Now that the bureau has been ordered to be abolished, all matters relating to the official properties in the four counties are under the jurisdiction of the respective county governments. The magistrate of Wuxian County received the provincial order and specially sent Section Member Li to the bureau yesterday to take over all the files and equipment.

County Anti-Smoking Association Builds a Prison

The Wuxian County Anti-Smoking Committee has been handling smoking cases in recent months and has detained more than 200 smoking offenders. They are being held separately in the county government's Public Security Bureau detention center and the Land Rent Office sub-office. There is a feeling of overcrowding. In the future, when dealing with compulsory detoxification and abstinence ceremonies, it will inevitably be more crowded. It is necessary to build another prison. Therefore, the association decided to build a prison, which will cost about 20,000 yuan. It is planned to use the license fee item for expenditure. Yesterday (3rd), a plan was drafted and submitted to the provincial anti-smoking committee member Zeng for review. Construction will begin as soon as it is approved.

Wuxi: Trouble Caused by Competing to Buy Silkworm Eggs

This year's spring silkworm eggs in Jiangsu Province are being shipped to Zhejiang Province in large numbers, resulting in a shortage of silkworm eggs in this province and causing great panic. In this county, only two or three out of ten villagers have been able to purchase silkworm eggs, and most have not been able to purchase them, which has a great impact on rural areas. The silkworm demonstration area in this county ordered 30,000 sheets of silkworm eggs from Japan. After they were transported to Wuxi, in addition to a portion being transported to Changzhou, Yixing, Jiangyin, Yangzhong, and other counties, Wuxi was allocated 18,000 sheets. In addition to the 11,000 sheets that had already been reserved, there were still 7,000 sheets, which were distributed by the demonstration area to the Wuxi Hotel, Dadong Hotel, and New Hotel, and other silkworm egg sales points on the road, limited to sale at 9:00 a.m. yesterday (3rd). The demonstration area also sent personnel to supervise. However, it was a drop in the bucket and did not help, and the villagers were in urgent need. At dawn, they went to wait for the sale on an empty stomach. There were no less than several thousand people. When it came to the sale, everyone scrambled to be first, and the old and weak could not buy them and were squeezed. At that time, the noise was deafening, and the order was chaotic. Then there were many rogues who saw the opportunity and rushed forward to grab the silkworm eggs, resulting in great chaos. The situation was serious. The counter glass windows of the Dadong Hotel were all damaged. The Wuxi Hotel closed the iron gate tightly to avoid being damaged. Later, the demonstration area reported the situation to the county government, which ordered the security team police to the scene to maintain order. The rogues who caused the incident had already fled. Only seven villagers, Shen Jusheng, Hua Panlin, Zhang Genfa, Gu Heshang, Ni Aixiu, Zhang Fenzu, and Zhu Weixuan, were taken to the second sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau and sent to the General Bureau for investigation. Now, the demonstration area is extremely panicked due to the shortage of species and is properly seeking relief.

Major Robbery and Assault Case Occurs in Downtown Area

The day before yesterday (2nd), at around 6:00 p.m., a major robbery and assault case suddenly occurred at Zhang Yuchang Rice Shop in Huangni Bee outside the South Gate. Residents bravely captured three robbers. The details have been briefly recorded in this newspaper's telegram. It is now known that Zhang Yuchang Rice Shop, which was robbed, has been open for 30 years. The owner's name is Zhang Xiufang. Recently, he purchased 56 and a half dan of coarse japonica rice from Yuan He Tian Rice Shop, worth 531 yuan. At around 5:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, Yuan He sent a clerk, Shen Qingrong, to the shop to collect the money. Zhang Xiufang's son, Lanchen, checked the accounts with Shen at the counter and took out 300 yuan in banknotes from the table in preparation for delivery. At that moment, a robber suddenly rushed into the counter, first pushed Shen Qingrong to the ground, and then searched the 300 yuan in banknotes on the table and put them into a bag. There were two more robbers, each holding a pistol, guarding the door. Seeing that the goal had been achieved, they fired a shot as a warning. Fortunately, no one was injured. The three robbers then fled toward Huangniqiao. Seeing that the robbers had left, the shop immediately reported to the police station and sent police to search for them. At the same time, the shop's apprentice, Zhu Jubao, and the shop clerk, Ren Ajiu, bravely chased after the robbers, shouting loudly. The neighbors heard the sound and rushed out, gathering more and more people to help chase the robbers. Seeing that the situation was not good, the robbers turned back and fired two shots, but the crowd still chased after them relentlessly. The robbers ran wildly through the downtown area, as if they were in a no-man's land. The patrol police along the way, because they were unarmed, did not dare to stop them. When they reached the corner next to a small silk factory, one robber hit the wall and fell to the ground, but he still got up and ran away, firing continuously. When they fled to Yao Lane, a resident, Ren [illegible], heard the noise and came out to watch. As soon as she stepped out of the gate, she was shot in the right waist by a stray bullet from the robber and fell to the ground immediately, bleeding profusely and unconscious. She was immediately sent to Puren Hospital for treatment, and her life is in critical condition. Afterwards, the robbers continued to fire more than ten shots, but the crowd was still chasing them, and the sound of gongs and police sirens rang out. They also threw stones at the robbers. A robber named Wang Xisheng had his head broken by a stone and was kicked to the ground by Wang Jinfu, who was catching the robbers. The robber was captured, and a Browning pistol was seized. Afterwards, Zhao Yun and others, who were catching the robbers, captured two more robbers, You Guozhen and Xu Jinlin, one after another, and seized another pistol and three bullets. The three robbers were tied up with ropes and sent to the third sub-bureau for questioning. They confessed to the robbery. It was decided that they would be sent to the county for trial today. It is also known that Nanli Township Chief Wang Jiehui and others specially convened a Baojia meeting yesterday to discuss security issues and submitted a request to the authorities for awards to be given to the villagers who captured the robbers with their bare hands.

Department Orders Reduction of Dry Cocoon Freight Rates

Wuxi Yongtai Silk Factory, due to the slump in the silk market and the decreasing number of local cocoons in Wuxi, which affected the raw materials for silk production, specially organized Tongyi Company to purchase fresh cocoons from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Shandong, Hubei, and other provinces, dry them, and transport them to Wuxi. The Chamber of Commerce sent telegrams to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Railways, requesting that this dry cocoon be exempted from transit tax when passing through customs and that freight rates be reduced in order to reduce costs and maintain the silk industry, which is on the verge of collapse. Yesterday, an order was received from the Ministry of Finance stating that the transit tax had been submitted by the department for abolition and would be implemented on a regular basis. All requests for the issuance of dry cocoon passports were not approved. At the same time, an order was received from the Ministry of Railways stating that the request to reduce dry [cocoon] freight rates had been referred to the Jinpu, Jiaoji, Longhai, Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo, Pinghan, and Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureaus. They replied that dry cocoon freight rates had already been reduced to the third class, and the minimum amount for full-car shipments had been changed from one-third to one-half of the vehicle's carrying capacity. In addition, there are progressive distance reduction methods for reported joint transportation. Compared to the past, it has already been reduced a lot, and there is no need to reduce it further. However, it was found that there was no road transportation of dry cocoons from Qingzhou to Wuxi, and the freight rate for sea transportation via Qingdao was unknown and difficult to investigate at one time. If it is indeed lower than the railway, the merchant can collect and submit the proof documents, and they will be reviewed in detail and appropriately reduced to attract business. They should be directly submitted to the railway for verification and decision.

Changzhou: Two Criminals Arrested in Kidnapping Case of Liu Hangsu

Liu Hangsu, the second son of the late painter Liu Quran of Wuyi, Dongxiatang, went to Xizizhou on January 13th of this year to collect rent and was kidnapped by bandits. There has been no news of him. It has been more than three months. The bandits knew that a party member, Luan Dechun, had recently been sent to Changzhou to negotiate ransom matters. The Liu family hired a certain Chan to negotiate with him. As a result, they agreed to pay a ransom of 5,000 yuan, but at that time, due to difficulties in raising funds, it was not resolved. Unexpectedly, the bandit Yue Dechun recently had a fight with someone in Maqiao, Taixing, and was captured by the Maqiao Self-Defense Corps and temporarily detained. Upon hearing the news, the Wuyi Detective Team went to pick him up and brought him to Changzhou the night before last. In addition, Chen Bojiu, the captain of the 3rd Security Team, arrested a bandit, Yin Hongda, at Qixigang at the same time and brought him to Changzhou. Both criminals have confessed to the kidnapping in the team. They were sent to the county government for interrogation on the 2nd.

Haimen: Bandits Attempt to Rob Shangsanhe Town

At around 6:00 p.m. yesterday (1st), eight or nine bandits suddenly arrived in Shangsanhe Town in the second district, intending to rob it. They were discovered by the merchants and residents of the town, who reported to the Public Security Sub-Station. Patrol Chief Gu led more than ten police officers to search and arrest them. Seeing that the situation was not good, the bandits opened fire to resist, wounding merchant Cai Boxian's right hand. They then scattered and fled. After the police officers tried their best to pursue them, they captured three bandits and seized a box gun and more than ten bullets. The remaining bandits escaped without a trace. That night, the sub-station sent the three bandits and guns to the county government for interrogation.

Confiscation of Firearms Being Smuggled

Recently, robbery cases have occurred frequently in the villages of this county. The firearms and bullets used by the bandits are secretly transported from Shanghai to Haimen. Therefore, the police teams in each port have been strictly inspecting disembarking passengers. Yesterday morning, a passenger with a local accent came to Haimen from Shanghai by boat. He disembarked from Qinglonggang. When he walked to Sanchang Town, a patrol officer saw that his appearance was suspicious and stopped him for inspection. Five pistols were found on his waist. The person and the stolen goods were taken to the bureau and sent to the county government for interrogation.

Yangzhou: The Puqi Road Disturbance Subsides

The Construction Bureau of this county, having been ordered to construct the Yangjing section of Puqi Road, commenced work on April 30th. The construction recently reached the Wanglou Township and Xiannv Temple in the fourth district. Unexpectedly, when work began on April 30th, a portion of the populace, failing to understand the importance of the project, requested that construction be postponed until after the wheat harvest. This led to a gathering of people obstructing the work, creating a disturbance. Liu Zhaorong, the head of the fourth district, considered the matter significant and immediately telegraphed the county government's Construction Bureau to request instructions. County Magistrate Ma promptly ordered Construction Bureau Chief Shu Guohua and Public Security Bureau Chief Zhang to rush to the scene to handle the situation. After arriving at Xiannv Temple, they immediately convened a meeting with the heads of all townships and towns in the district, informing them that the road was being constructed under strict orders from the capital and province, with a deadline for completion that could not be delayed. Regarding the wheat in the fields, approval had been obtained from the Construction Department to provide reasonable compensation. Every effort would be made to resolve any losses to the people's land. He hoped that the township and town heads would inform the populace not to be manipulated by a few individuals. The villagers, realizing that they could not resist, resumed work in sections that very afternoon and aimed to complete the project by May 10th.

Jisheng Society Distributes Disaster Relief Funds in Disaster Areas

Due to the exceptionally severe drought in the western mountains of this county, the China Jisheng Society dispatched representatives to Yiju Ji, Chenjia Ji, Liujia Ji, Xiejia Ji, Tiepai Dian, Gujing Temple, and other locations in the eighth district to investigate the disaster conditions. They selected households severely affected by the disaster and distributed relief tickets. The investigation has now been completed, and it has been decided to distribute relief funds according to the ticket denominations on the 4th and 5th at Tianning Temple. All sectors were also notified in advance to arrive at the venue on time to supervise the distribution.

Nantong: Wireless Radio Station Established in Tongcheng

To facilitate the implementation of government orders in the northern Jiangsu counties, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has established a wireless radio station in Tongcheng. Receiving and transmitting equipment has already been transported via the Shanjin Tianlun steamer. The radio station will be attached to the Nantong District Administrative Inspector's Office. The provincial government will subsidize 60% of the monthly expenses, with the remaining funds to be raised by the commissioner.

Opening Ceremony Held Yesterday Morning: Over a Thousand Students and Citizens Attended

Xinsheng News Agency reports that the Student National Goods Year Promotion Federation held the opening ceremony of the Seventh District National Goods Exhibition at Tongji Vocational Middle School in Jiangwan at 9 AM yesterday. In addition to representatives from various agencies and organizations, Mayor Wu (represented by Pan Gongzhan), Pan Gongzhan, Tong Xingbai, Chen Jicheng, Wang Zhongming, Yan Zhengqing, Yang Weiyu, Tang Ying, and others, as well as students from ten schools, including Xinmin Middle School, Lida College, Tongji Vocational Middle School, Yuqing Middle School, Hongjiang Middle School, Jiangxi Elementary School, and Xinmin Commercial School, and approximately one thousand citizens attended.

A Glimpse of the Venue

The general assembly was held at the affiliated vocational school of Tongji University at Jiangwan Station. The national flag and the Party flag were hung at the main entrance, along with a banner reading "Shanghai Student National Goods Year Promotion Federation National Student Supplies Exhibition." The exhibition and the platform were set up in the auditorium. Boy Scouts from Xinmin and Lida Middle Schools were responsible for maintaining order at the venue and the entrance. Exquisite products from various national goods factories were displayed at the venue, and a sales department was attached. The arrangement was extremely exquisite. On the left and right sides, eye-catching cartoons and slogans promoting the use of national goods were posted everywhere.

Slogans

In order to promote the concept of using national goods among students and citizens, the conference particularly shouted slogans: "1. We students are the vanguard of using national goods. 2. We must be responsible for persuading the entire society to use national goods. 3. We must promote the manufacture of national goods. 4. We must promote the sales of national goods. 5. Using national goods is cultivating national strength. 6. Using national goods is solving the livelihood problems of the entire nation." Slogans were also posted everywhere, such as "Use domestic products of our own country to seek self-reliance," "Using national goods can increase the national economy," "Those who buy foreign goods are ashamed even if they are rich," "Use your own strength to seek self-reliance," and "Using domestic products of our own country can save the country," etc.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony was performed, Tong Xingbai of the presidium first reported, "Dear students, dear guests, today is the opening ceremony of the National Goods Year Promotion Federation's Seventh District National Student Supplies Exhibition. Not long ago, we held a city-wide student oath ceremony to use national goods. I believe everyone present has participated. The significance of this district exhibition lies in material, because the significance of the last oath ceremony lay in spirit. Therefore, we are now using material to supplement the lack of spirit, so as to strengthen the concept of using national goods. General exhibitions are mostly held in cities, so this time we are holding it in rural areas, so that citizens and students in rural areas can have the opportunity to thoroughly understand national goods. Therefore, we deeply hope that students and citizens in the seventh district can cherish this exhibition, which has great significance. There are two meanings to holding it in rural areas this time. First, to enable people in rural areas to see various exquisite national goods, so that they can make a comparison with foreign goods. Second, to enable the people to see national goods and then trigger the concept of using national goods. Therefore, I hope that after you visit the exhibition, you can immediately resolve to use national goods and persuade relatives and friends to use national goods." Then, Wang Zhongming of the presidium reported on the preparations, and Chen Jicheng, a representative of the University Faculty and Staff Association, and Cao Zhigong, a representative of the National Goods Factory, made speeches.

Grand Event

After the ceremony, they visited the exhibition. Xiangshi Chinese and French Pharmacy, Tianzhang Paper Mill, Aihua Pharmaceutical Company, Weiyi Specialty Manufacturing Factory, and others specially presented exquisite products. At the same time, each factory in the sales department sold various exquisite products at discounted prices. Visitors were able to purchase inexpensive and beautiful national goods. It was also heard that in order to arouse the interest of visitors and to enable them to have a deeper understanding of national goods, the association specially collected manufacturing process films from various national goods factories and screened them from 7 PM to 9 PM in the evening. Anyone who purchased more than two jiao of goods in the sales department would receive an admission ticket. If national goods manufacturers are willing to lend the films, please send them to the association's office at No. 80 Longhua Road, etc.

Song Ziwen Discusses Matters Related to Three Banks' Relief to Industry and Commerce; Russian Ambassador Visited Yesterday for General Courtesy; Bank of China to Expand Deposit Savings

Central News Agency reports that Song Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council and Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Bank of China, received reporters from various newspapers at the Shanghai Office of the Economic Council on West Adams Road at 5 PM yesterday and spoke freely about matters related to the three banks' relief to industry and commerce. The various situations are divided as follows:

Meeting with the Soviet Russian Ambassador

Song met with Soviet Russian Ambassador Bogomolov at his private residence on Sheqi Road at 4 PM yesterday. The discussion lasted for half an hour. After Ambassador Bao resigned, he immediately met with reporters from various newspapers. According to Song, Ambassador Bao's visit to him was purely for ordinary courtesy and did not involve political issues between the two countries.

Relief Funds for Industry and Commerce

Regarding the issue of the three banks providing relief to industry and commerce, Song replied to reporters' questions that the decline of industry and commerce really urgently needs relief. It has been decided that the Central, China, and Communications Banks will allocate 20 million yuan for loans. Finance Minister Kong is in charge of this matter. As far as he knows, a 5 million yuan small loan for industrial and commercial credit will be established first, and it is now being actively carried out. As for the money borrowed by the three banks, more than 10 million yuan has been released by the end of last week, etc.

Expand Deposit Savings

The articles of association of the Bank of China have been revised, and it has now been decided to expand deposit savings, which has been approved by the Ministry of Finance and will be implemented immediately. The branches of the Bank of China are all over the mainland, so after the expansion of deposit savings, considerable achievements can definitely be obtained. Bian Fusheng has been decided to be the director of the savings department. Song then said that after the expansion of savings matters, the power to relieve the countryside will also inevitably increase, because according to the bank savings law, one-fifth of the deposit savings should be withdrawn and invested in rural relief matters. Therefore, the Bank of China will pay more attention to rural economic relief work in the future and hopes to make every effort to carry it out, so that rural finance will gradually develop. The examination of the reports on the achievements of various banks investing in rural areas has proved that lending to rural areas is better than lending to cities, because borrowers in the interior have land and industry as collateral, which is very stable and reliable, and cannot be compared with huge urban companies that open in the morning and close in the evening. Regarding this level, not only the Bank of China pays attention to it, but all banks also express sympathy.

His mission is twofold: first, to draft various laws and regulations for the Legislative Yuan and to investigate the people's conditions; and second, to handle the affairs of the National Economic Council, because Sun is also one of the standing committee members of the Economic Council. Therefore, during Sun's trip, all matters related to the Economic Council that urgently need to be investigated will be investigated one by one. His itinerary includes the northwestern provinces, Qinghai, and other areas, but it will be very short. As for British railway rights holder Brigadier General Edmund, who came to China to investigate our country's railway system, he was hired by our government and not by the Economic Council. Hai is expected to arrive in Shanghai around the 5th.

Accidents Involving Northern Shipping Lines: Lisheng Grounded, Beikang Collides

Lisheng Grounded at Gukou

The Yih and Company Northern Line regular liner Lisheng loaded cargo and passengers from Tianjin this time and set sail from Tianjin on the night of the first of this month. Guided by a pilot, it left the Baihe River to Dagukou to go to sea, first to Zhifu, and then to Shanghai. The ship sailed to Dagukou on the 2nd (Thursday). Because the pilot went the wrong channel, the Lisheng's hull was grounded on the shallow sand at Dagukou. The Lisheng had a deeper draft and was heavily loaded, causing the hull to be trapped in the shallow sand and unable to escape.

Beikang Collides on Entry

The Northern Shipping Company's Beikang, with a deadweight of 1,013 tons, was loading a large batch of flour and groceries in Shanghai this time and sailed to Dagu on the morning of the 2nd of this month. While entering Gukou, the Lisheng was already grounded at Dagukou, and its grounded position was at the key point of the Dagukou's shipping route for entry and exit. When the Beikang entered Dagukou, its hull collided with the Lisheng. The bows and outer sides of both ships were damaged.

Reporting the Situation to Shanghai

Yesterday, Yih and Company and the Northern Company both received telegrams from Tianjin reporting that after the stranded Lisheng collided with the Beikang, they had reported to the Tianjin Customs and sent personnel to inspect the ships. On the one hand, the shipowners telegraphed Shanghai to report. Now the company has telegraphed the law firm to send a ship to tow it out when the tide rises. The damage situation is unknown, but it is generally not obstructing navigation and can still come to Shanghai. The ship was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 7th, but it is now inevitably postponed. How much damage there is will be inspected after arriving in Shanghai. The Beikang has also telegraphed Shanghai to inform them.

Notification to Insurance Company

The Northern Company obtained a telegram from the Beikang yesterday and immediately informed the relevant insurance company, briefly stating that it had received a telegram from the Beikang stating that the Lisheng was grounded at Gukou and the Beikang collided with the Lisheng when entering the river (i.e., entering Dagukou). The rest will be detailed in a letter, etc. Yesterday afternoon, a reporter from this newspaper went to the Northern Company to inquire. It was said that the wording of the collision was extremely simple and it was still impossible to know everything in detail. The situation will only be clear after a follow-up telegram arrives in Shanghai.

Silver and Money Industry and Three Banks to Discuss Implementation of Relief Loans; Funds Approved by the Money Industry to be Collected in Preparation

After the Shanghai industry and commerce passed the end of April, most of the credit loans and mortgage loans that were due were extended. The added water has also declined, which proves that the money supply in Shanghai has gradually eased.

Page 10

Literacy Movement Week Business Day: City Chamber of Commerce Issues Letter to Merchants

Yesterday was the business promotion day for the literacy education promotion week in this city. The City Chamber of Commerce issued a letter to merchants, stating that the authorities in this city, in order to relieve the illiterate people in the urban area, have decided to organize compulsory literacy education for one year, from July 1, 1935, to June 30, 1936. The method is that the literacy education committee currently organized in this city will establish hundreds of literacy schools starting from July 1 this year, compelling illiterate people to go to school in batches for one hour a day for two months. Employers of store employees or workers have an obligation to facilitate the above-mentioned classes. The current procedures are to start with the committee investigating the illiterate people on a household-by-shop basis. The significance of the promotion week is to try to make the general public understand the importance of literacy education and create a warm and strong interest in literacy education, so that the literacy education organized in this city can be carried out smoothly. This is the origin of the business community for organizing literacy education in this city and the significance of the promotion week that should be understood first. Secondly, what is the relationship between literacy education and merchants? In other words, it is the center of this problem, that is, the purpose of this association issuing a letter to merchants this time. The merchants in our country have always had a fundamental misconception that once a merchant enters a store, business is important and reading is light. There are very few apprentices who are studious and study on their own in their spare time, and there are none who are not reprimanded by the shopkeeper. Some even say that the rise and establishment of previous generations all came from practical training, and they never made a living on paper. These remarks originally had considerable reasons when used in the self-sufficient commerce of the closed era, but since the world is open and the power of foreign economic oppression has increased day by day, no matter what industry, one must be familiar with economic principles and understand the news of foreign markets to plan a response. Literacy education is the tool to know economic principles and understand foreign news. Therefore, the purpose of organizing literacy education is not to create useless bookworms for the business community, but to create a healthy merchant for the business war era who can fight when advancing and defend when retreating. In order to achieve this goal, the current literacy education is only implementing the initial stage. Generally, a company or a store is an entire organization in nature. From the manager to the employees, if there is an unsound member, there will inevitably be some shortcomings in the operation of the business. Therefore, in recent years, shopkeepers who understand things and stores with larger scales have all set up employee tutoring education. Even if they do not run employee tutoring education themselves, they often reward the extracurricular tutoring of employees and apprentices and do not hinder them. This is enough to prove that the importance of allowing illiterate merchants to make up for their studies has gradually been understood by the general public. This is something that store owners have mutually beneficial benefits, and I hope that the general store owners will not misunderstand that it hinders store affairs. Furthermore, the concept of merchants in our country has always been that store owners regard partners as guests and hosts, and store owners regard apprentices as masters and brothers. There is almost no one who does not hope that they will be successful in the future and glorify the village. This kind of public and universal mind is really the virtue that our country has passed down from ancient times. Therefore, encouraging them to make up for their illiteracy, so that they can increase their commercial knowledge, so as to be able to establish themselves in the future, is even more the obligation that today's store owners and managers should have. I hope that the general merchants in this city will understand this meaning.

Wang Guoxiu's Thoughts

Mr. Wang Guoxiu published his thoughts in the China Review Weekly yesterday. The original title was Chinese Influence On English Porcelain And Furniture. His insights are incisive and his writing is fluent. The main points are excerpted and translated as follows: Since the establishment of the East India Company, the trade between China and England has developed extremely rapidly. Among the decorations exported by China, porcelain ranks first and lacquerware ranks second. In the 18th century, British women mostly placed tea tables, flower vases, and porcelain vases at home. Between the 17th and 18th centuries, the British built kilns in England to make porcelain. However, the raw materials for this porcelain mostly came from overseas, and they initially imitated the styles of Chinese porcelain, and they liked to use oriental blue and white ware as the style. The Kangxi kiln and Qianlong kiln in this preview, such as the blue and white awl arch chrysanthemum petal flower sprinkler No. 226 and the white banana leaf thunder pattern jue imitating the Ding kilns No. 248, were the styles in the 18th century that the British used as models. Also, the enamel color yellow ground tangled peony pattern, and the white awl arch cloud bat string pattern pot imitating the Ding kilns No. 246, were also the items that British women loved to play with most in the 18th century. Later, the Bow Worcester and Chelsea factories in England manufactured fine porcelain, but their styles and colors still used Chinese porcelain as the standard. The porcelain is mostly painted with Chinese landscape figures, flowers, and birds. The porcelain No. 239 enamel color bamboo and sparrow garden wine bell, the blue and white fish dragon transformation large wash No. 194, and the enamel color hundred flower land open light blue material landscape handle in this preview were all the things that the British envied most at that time. Porcelain makers thought they were imitating them. As for lacquerware, it was also a decoration for wealthy British families. The ones made in England were completely imitated Chinese styles. The No. 1 gold footrest in the furniture category in this preview reminds people of the utensils used in England in the 18th century. However, the development of lacquerware making in England is not as developed as porcelain making. After that, the interest of the British in using Chinese furniture gradually decreased, but in the history of British art, we can still see the influence of China.

Ge Zhi Public School Textbook: "Manchukuo" Scraped off Maps

The Ge Zhi Public School, established by the Public Works Department, previously used geography maps that included the term "Manchukuo." Consequently, the school's students, believing this violated the League of Nations' resolution denying recognition of the puppet state of Manchukuo, requested the school authorities to replace them. Subsequently, the school's vice-principal immediately collected the sold maps from the students, issuing each a receipt pending further action. It is now reported that on the day before yesterday (the 2nd), the school clerk, acting on the principal's orders, announced that the maps had been revised and that students could claim them from the office upon presentation of their receipts. It is learned that the school had used a knife to scrape off the words "Manchukuo" "Nlonchukuo" and "國 Kuo" from the maps before returning them.

Telephone Bureau: Director Xu Returns to Shanghai from Sichuan After Completing Official Duties

The Ministry of Communications considered Yichang to be an important town in Western Hubei, a major trading port. The commercially operated Qingxin Telephone Company there was corrupt and incompetent. Therefore, it ordered Xu Xueyu, Director of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau, to go there to take over and reorganize the company, with a deadline of completion by April. Director Xu led his staff to Yichang on February 17th and established a preparatory office on the 18th to begin work. Because the machinery and equipment were old and dilapidated, and the poles and lines were rusty, it was impossible to reorganize them. Therefore, it was decided to completely replace them. At the same time, negotiations were conducted to take over the company. However, it was during the Lunar New Year holiday, the water level was low, and the cables and equipment were bulky and difficult to transport, resulting in delays. In addition, there were no poles available locally for purchase, so staff had to be sent to Hankou to procure them. Going upstream was difficult, and loading and transporting them was a challenge. All the equipment finally arrived in Yichang on March 22nd. Construction began on January 28th, and after working day and night, it was completed and put into operation on April 5th. The sound was clear and distinct, the connections were quick, and the users were very satisfied. The entire project took only 36 days. All the old poles and lines of the commercial company were leaning and disorderly, which was unsightly, so they were dismantled to improve the appearance of the city. The work has now been completed, and it was handed over to the Yichang Telegraph Bureau on April 28th. The Ministry of Communications also considered Chengdu to be the capital of Sichuan Province, and telephone communications were very important during the current period of bandit suppression. Therefore, Director Xu was again sent to the west to inspect and design improvements, including the installation of a 1,000-line common battery switchboard. Having completed his official duties, it is reported that all staff, except for a portion of the line workers who were transferred to Chengdu, are scheduled to return to Shanghai in early May to prepare the machinery, equipment, and tools needed for Chengdu.

Leather and Silk Tobacco Industry Association: Telegraphs Fujian Province to Stop Collecting Business Tax

The Shanghai Leather and Silk Tobacco Industry Association telegraphed the Fujian Provincial Finance Department on April 28th, stating: "To Xu Jun, Director of the Fujian Provincial Finance Department: Since Yongding tobacco silk has already paid the special tax, it should not be subject to business tax again. We await your command with utmost urgency. The Shanghai Leather and Silk Tobacco Industry Association bows."

City Chamber of Commerce Submits to Ministry of Finance: Request to Exempt Leather Export Tax

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "Re: Request. On the 1st of this month, the Leather, Fur, Oil, and Bone Trade Association sent a letter stating that animal hides are divided into wild and domestic animals. Wild animals include tigers, leopards, foxes, deer, raccoon dogs, wildcats, field mice, and weasels, which are produced in open fields or hidden in valleys. Domestic animals include lake sheep and rabbits, which are raised by villagers in gardens. Every winter, when farming is done, farmers switch from farming to hunting, slaughtering animals for their hides to sell and supplement their livelihoods. The above-mentioned hides are not used domestically and are entirely sold abroad. Exports have been substantial for many years. Therefore, the hides industry benefits the national economy and people's livelihoods to a great extent. In recent years, it has been subject to competition from dumping by Japan and Russia, and has been affected by the global economic panic and the increase in the price of silver. As a result, the sales of Chinese animal hides have declined daily, and the market price has plummeted. Not only have inland vendors and urban leather merchants suffered losses and found it difficult to survive, but the value obtained by farmers selling their hides has been insufficient to cover the cost of hunting or the cost of feed. If this continues without any effort to save the industry, hunting will inevitably cease in the wild, and merchants will stop trading in the market. The elimination of China's hide export industry is imminent. The harm to the national economy and people's livelihoods is immeasurable. Japan and Russia provide comprehensive protection for the hide industry, such as establishing ranches, increasing production, and exempting export taxes to facilitate exports. They also have incentive measures for hide exporters. Therefore, Japanese and Russian hides have no fear in the European and American markets and are dumped in large quantities. The increase in sales over the years has been rapid. On the other hand, Chinese hides are burdened by heavy export tariffs, and inland transportation is difficult, with costs increasing due to multiple transfers by boats and vehicles. Due to various factors, the cost is higher. Compared to Japanese and Russian goods, the difference is like heaven and earth. China's trade deficit in recent years has been alarming. The only thing that helps is the export of domestic goods to offset it. However, since overseas countries have raised the price of silver, Chinese exports have been greatly hit. The hide industry relies on exports, so it is the first to be affected. The impact is immeasurable. The association has witnessed the crisis and cannot remain silent. Therefore, we present the facts and request that your association forward them to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to exempt all kinds of animal hides from export tariffs and quickly devise fundamental policies to save farmers and merchants in order to maintain a portion of the vitality of the country. We await your command with utmost urgency." The association also noted that the export sales of raw and tanned hides in the past year decreased by nearly 90% compared to 1933. In order to maintain trade balance and encourage import and export trade, it is necessary to reduce or exempt taxes. Reports indicate that the Ministry is preparing to abolish all transit taxes and is considering reducing or exempting export taxes based on trade conditions. The circumstances described by the industry are consistent with the Ministry's current proposed reduction or exemption standards. Based on the foregoing, we respectfully submit this report and request that your Ministry review and approve the association's request for the sake of public convenience.

Apprehension of Robbers: Incidentally Uncovered a Fraud Case

Liu Junxiang, a Chinese detective of the Laozha Police Station, along with detective inspectors Pang Ruiqing and He Xuezhi, learned that Gu Fengshan, a robber from Haimen who had robbed property from No. 55, Lane 107, Parker Road, was hiding in Room 7 of the Zhonghe Hotel, Lane 150, Fujian Road. Therefore, at 11:30 AM on the day before yesterday, they reported to Chief Chinese Detective You Aji and went to the address to arrest him. Unexpectedly, a fraud case was also uncovered. Gu Fengshan and his friends Zhang Lianfu from Chongming, Shen Zijiang from Haimen, and Yang Peiran from Shaoxing, etc., stayed in Room 16 of the Lin'an Hotel, Lane 108, Guangdong Road, on the 29th of last month. The next morning, they discovered that clothing worth more than 40 yuan had been stolen. They negotiated with the hotel without success. They then ordered Hu Sanqing, the owner of the Lin'an Hotel, to go to the Zhonghe Hotel and force them to pay 46 yuan. After repeated negotiations, Hu handed over 20 yuan, the banknotes of which were marked with secret marks, and Zhang Lianfu received them. At this time, police detectives arrived and arrested Liu and the other three people. The original stolen 20 yuan was found on Zhang, and a pawn ticket from Yufeng Pawnshop was found on Gu Fengshan. The item pawned was a diamond ring robbed from Parker Road. They were all taken back to the police station. The victims came to identify them, but none could identify them. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu explained the situation and filed a lawsuit under Article 318, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law for the crime of obstructing freedom. However, due to the need for further investigation, he requested permission to postpone the hearing. After a brief interrogation by Judge Huang Risheng, he ordered them to be returned to custody for further interrogation at a later date. According to the police investigation, Gu Fengshan, also known as Sha Bangcai, is actually a recidivist from Qidong County who has committed many crimes and was wanted by the local security bureau but had not been apprehended.

River Bend Welcoming God Race Meeting: Burning of Idol Incident

Merchants Present City Chamber of Commerce Presiding Public Justice, Fire Brigade Submitted Truth to Authority

Huadong News reports that the River Bend Welcoming God Race Meeting, vulgarly called Rolling River Bend, sees no fewer than 100,000 people participating in the parade each year. Due to maintaining order, an idol-burning incident happened. Recently, the merchants and people of River Bend have presented the City Chamber of Commerce to ask it to preside over justice, and to stop paying subsidies to the River Bend Fire Brigade. The citizens are also extremely dissatisfied. There are even those with black armbands to show grief at the idols being destroyed who have been attacked with an axe. Mao Alang, who bangs the head gong, has petitioned the District Court to strictly punish the murderer. The River Bend Fire Brigade has also reported the incident to Police Chief Cai of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, reporting the event's progress. Divided in left:

Fire Brigade Report to Public Security Bureau

The common ignorant citizens of River Bend,

Municipal Party Department Strictly Forbids Welcoming God Race Meetings Sends Letter to Municipal Government for Public Order Ban

This Municipality's City Party Department, taking that the Welcoming God Race Meeting, must not involve superstition, and is instead an effort to move people and waste wealth, now in this promotion of the new life movement, should be strictly forbidden, therefore it has been in two letters to the Municipal Public Security Bureau asking for a ban. Recently Pudong River Bend again has this action happening, Zhabei is even brewing it, if the whole city goes wild then without strict banning, we fear at this point in May with serious social disorder, that petty thieves will take the opportunity to mingle in. The original letter is as follows: Direct announcement is as follows: Having investigated Welcoming God Race Meetings, moving people and wasting wealth, bad habits and deteriorating customs, should be prohibited on this grounds. Now the nearby Pudong Welcomed Gods first, then River Bend has a Race Meeting later. Promoting superstition is the most extreme, ruining the new movement, there is nothing more so. The City Party Department has twice written a letter to the Public Security Bureau asking for a ban. Originally it was to smash superstition, make customs beautiful, prevent disorder, to stop conflicts. Unfortunately, the previous letter spoke truthfully. On April 30th River Bend Race Meeting, aroused the general antipathy. As a result, the on-site fire brigade members used the opportunity of maintaining order, and so in the evening after the masses had scattered, they set fire to the wooden figures on display, to root out the superstition, this action was not only to the heart's great joy, and also did not arouse incident, the timing of the treatment was especially appropriate. Having investigated River Bend Liu Shrine Three Sages, names are recorded in the biography. Especially Mr. Liu Pingshan was a great scholar in Song, a famous family for logical study. For the alien races' creeds, he purged them most strongly while alive. By building a shrine here, as people look up and emulate, to take as standard for later generations, this Welcoming God Race Meeting is no less than to take Mr. Liu's evil hatred of things done while he was alive, to add them to his body today, is it not to defile the former sage, is it really against building the shrine to respect his will, local government should take care of the forebearer, correct mistaken beliefs. They in fact let the big shot seduce and fool the masses, so that they can found the basis of a feudal evil force, it is truly regrettable. Shanghai is where the world is looking, the source of cultural promotion, its rumors spread, the whole country follows, now that the New Life Movement is actively progressing, but the Welcoming God Race Meetings, which were prohibited for more than a decade, simultaneously spring up, one advocates, the other harmonizes, the whole city goes mad, can it be that we do not doubt whether foreigners call our New Life Movement so, or even that this matter is such, if Shanghai is like this, will there be others who do not hear of it and rise up? The City Party Department seeing the future of culture and the New Movement, cannot but tremble. Shortly according to reports, the Zhabei Every Heaven Society is again preparing, local hooligans and thugs have been going door to door to swindle money. If it is let go any further, and it is at this time in May with serious disorder, its harms are unpredictable. So it is especially writing this letter to your Government, asking for a quick announcement and a strict order for the Public Security Bureau to take responsibility for the ban. For those who dare to start Welcoming God Race Meeting incidents again, it is immediately to arrest the person in charge, all the disputes caused by the Welcoming God Race Meeting, do not allow debating on who is right and who is wrong, if the person in charge and etcetera is to be questioned, he should be dealt with severely to straighten the morals, then the future of culture and the New Movement will be truly and deeply reliant. Also hoping that your Government will reply on the treatment's state of affairs, to the highest public friendship, this is addressed to the Shanghai Municipal Government.

Issue 11: Aviation Lottery Results Announced Yesterday

First Prize Number is 189207, Rumored to be Won in the Beiping-Tianjin Area

The eleventh drawing of the National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery was held at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Yiyuan Garden. Approximately two to three thousand Chinese and foreign individuals attended to observe. The drawing began promptly, and within twenty minutes, the first prize number "189207" was drawn. The Dayun Company reported they did not sell that ticket. It is speculated that the All-China Aviation Construction Association purchased it, as they acquired all remaining tickets this time. Details are provided below:

Venue Arrangement: The lottery drawing venue featured a large grandstand, with a canvas as a curtain at the front. The surroundings were decorated with intertwined Party and national flag emblems. A banner was hung with the words "The Eleventh National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Drawing is Held Here." A lottery drawing platform was set in the middle, with three copper balls labeled A, B, and C placed at the center. Blackboards were set on both sides to display the winning numbers. The front of the grandstand was reserved for committee members and reporters, while the rear was for guests. The entire venue was equipped with a broadcasting system to announce the winning numbers, transmitted through the system so the entire venue could hear. The office also contracted multiple broadcasting companies to broadcast in Chinese, English, French, and Russian to the whole city, allowing residents to listen to the report through their radios.

Supervision Representatives: The following individuals were present yesterday to supervise the lottery drawing: Luo Panhui, representative of Mayor Wu Tiecheng; Zhang Shouyong, representative of the Ministry of Finance; Lin Kanghou, representative of the Bankers Association; Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Ye Zhuotang, Hu Zutong, Xu Xinliu, committee members of the lottery office; and Chen Hong, director, and Chun Yin, secretary. Chinese and foreign attendees were even more enthusiastic, and the guest seating was full before 1:00 PM, with an estimated two to three thousand people present.

All Tickets Sold Out: The lottery tickets for this drawing were still sold by the Dayun Company in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces. Remote provinces were entrusted to local banks for sales or were sold directly by the office. The unsold and returned tickets were negotiated with the All-China Aviation Construction Association, which purchased all of them at face value. Therefore, all lottery tickets were sold this time, avoiding the troublesome procedure of drawing a special prize separately. This will be done similarly in the next drawing. According to committee member Du Yuesheng, the next lottery tickets are now on sale, and the procedures will remain unchanged.

Committee Report: At precisely 2:00 PM, after the lottery balls were inspected, committee member Wang Xiaolai announced that the drawing for the eleventh National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery was being held there today, and that all procedures had been inspected and completed. He then announced the start of the drawing, and also mentioned that all lottery tickets for this period had been sold out. This was followed by a message in English by Chen Hong, the director of the office.

First Prize Drawn: After the report, the steel balls were mixed, and the drawing began. Several fifth and sixth prizes were drawn first, approximately one hundred and ten in total. Then the first prize was drawn, being "189207". After the number was announced and broadcasted, the entire venue became tense, as attendees checked the numbers they held. Those who matched the last one or two digits and won eighth or ninth prizes looked joyful. It was reported that the first prize was won in the Beiping-Tianjin area.

Drawing of Seventh Prize: All other prizes were drawn by 4:00 PM. Then the seventh prize was drawn. Representatives present at the venue supervised as the wooden balls were poured into the A copper ball and mixed for several minutes. Then the number "100" was drawn for the seventh prize. All tickets with the last three digits matching this number won the prize. The fact that the number was exactly 100 was considered remarkable by the crowd, who cheered continuously. Other numbers, such as "277772," "232333," and "155555," were also considered quite unique, drawing laughter from the entire venue when reported.

Winning Numbers: The winning numbers for each prize are as follows: First prize (one): "185207"; Second prize (two): "129835" and "349583"; Third prize (four): "112388," "163185," "308536," and "482493"; Fourth prize (ten): "061721," "22016," "126362," "13438," "140741," "185930," "254120," "345149," "351586," and "493611"; Fifth and Sixth prizes (total 150): See the number list; Seventh prize: Last two digits "100"; Eighth prize: Last two digits "07"; Ninth prize: Last digit "7".

Prize Claim Date: According to the office's announcement, the prize claim period for the eleventh National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery, drawn publicly at Yiyuan Garden in Shanghai today, begins on May 11th of this year and ends on October 31st of this year. Prizes can be claimed at the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various locations. Unclaimed prizes after the deadline will be invalid. Special announcement, May 3, 24th year of the Republic of China, Director Chen Hong.

Next Issue on Sale: Tickets for the next lottery are now on sale, and the procedures remain the same. The drawing date is scheduled for July 5th at the same location. It has been reported that various lottery ticket vendors in Shanghai have proposed reducing the ticket price and changing the drawing to once a month to facilitate sales. Although the office has adopted the proposal and formulated a plan, it has not been approved by the Ministry of Finance. Therefore, the procedures for the next few issues will remain unchanged. However, some vendors intentionally raise the ticket price by one or two jiao per set on the morning of the drawing. Those responsible for sales should pay attention to this and stop it.

Women's Temperance Union Plans Mother's Day Celebration; Essay Contest Begins

The Chinese Women's Temperance Union at 206 Yuanmingyuan Road is busy preparing for Mother's Day on May 12th. Four resolutions were passed regarding Mother's Day celebration methods: (1) those without mothers should present flowers on stage; (2) those in distant locations should send letters of greetings, write essays praising maternal virtue, or donate to charitable organizations for causes that mothers would find most pleasing; (3) those who disobey their mothers should vow to correct their behavior; (4) those in the local area should use gifts, outings, parties, etc., to make their mothers happy. The union has also announced these methods, hoping that all sons and daughters, regardless of age, can immediately begin to act according to their individual circumstances.
